From: Security Team staff <STs@organization1.ol>
Organization: Organization1
To: CERT <cert@example_cert.org>
Subject: Suspicious Activity From 10.0.0.200
Date: Tue, 17 Abr 2013 10:10:28 +0200

Dear Sir,
This e-mail is to alert you that we have detected suspicious activity originating from the above IP address under your constituency (10.0.0.200), targeting one of our clients (172.16.3.24).

On Abr 17, 2013, from 20:00:00 to 10:00:00, we have detected a port scan attack coming from the above host. 

From 20:00:00 to 10:12:26 the scan was directed to the 80/tcp port (http) but after that, the attacker scan all the ports in the target machine looking for open services. This makes us think about the posibility of using a security/vulnerability scanner, firstly looking for well-known vulnerabilities in several cgi-bin scripts.

I attach logfiles from the attacker machine.

Please, forward this complaint to the appropiate security contact point in your constituency and get back to us when you have some feedback on it.

Note:
All times are reported in GMT+2.

Best regards,
Peter Perot

--
Peter Perot
Security Team staff in Organization1
Tel: +00 11 22 33 44  
e-mail: STs@organization1.ol
